Automatically classifies tasks into compliance tiers and enforces appropriate verification.\n\n**Key Benefits**:\n- Single command replaces confusion between `sc:task` and `sc:task-mcp`\n- Automatic tier classification with confidence scoring\n- Appropriate verification for each task type\n- Prevents over-engineering for trivial changes\n- Ensures safety for critical changes\n\n## Triggers\n\nUse `/sc:task` when:\n- Task involves code modifications with downstream impacts\n- Complexity score >0.6 with code modifications\n- Multi-file scope (>2 estimated affected files)\n- Security domain paths detected (auth/, security/, crypto/)\n- Refactoring or system-wide changes requested\n\n**Auto-Suggest Keywords**:\n- High confidence: \"implement feature\", \"refactor system\", \"fix security\", \"add authentication\", \"update database schema\"\n- Moderate confidence: \"add new\", \"create component\", \"update service\", \"modify API\"\n\n## Usage\n\n```bash\n/sc:task [description]                           # Auto-detect all dimensions\n/sc:task [description] --compliance strict       # Force STRICT tier\n/sc:task [description] --compliance light        # Force LIGHT tier\n/sc:task [description] --skip-compliance         # Bypass compliance (escape hatch)\n/sc:task [description] --verify auto             # Auto-select verification\n```\n\n## Behavioral Flow\n\n### 0. Load context via codebase-retrieval\n2. Search downstream impacts (find_referencing_symbols OR grep)\n3. Make changes\n4. Run affected tests OR document manual verification\n5. Verify basic functionality\n\n**LIGHT Execution**:\n1. Quick scope check (files/lines within bounds)\n2. Make changes\n3. Quick sanity check (syntax valid, no obvious errors)\n4. Proceed with judgment\n\n**EXEMPT Execution**:\n1. Execute immediately\n2. No verification overhead\n\n### 4. TodoWrite: Create task breakdown\n2. codebase-retrieval: Load context\n3. list_memories / read_memory: Check project state\n\n**Execution Phase**:\n1. Edit/MultiEdit/Write: Make changes\n2. Grep/Glob: Find references\n3. find_referencing_symbols: Trace dependencies\n\n**Verification Phase**:\n1. Task (quality-engineer): Spawn verification agent (STRICT only)\n2. Column names also differ (`Spec Quote`/`Roadmap Quote` vs `Upstream Quote`/`Downstream Quote`). Which schema is canonical?\n\n## Decision\n\n**The 7-column FR-051.4 schema is canonical. The `Source Pair` column is dropped from the table body and encoded in YAML frontmatter instead.**\n\n### Canonical 7-Column Schema\n\n| # | Column Name | Data Type | Description |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| 1 | ID | String | Unique deviation identifier (e.g., `DEV-001`) |\n| 2 | Severity | Enum | `HIGH` \\| `MEDIUM` \\| `LOW` |\n| 3 | Deviation | String | Description of the deviation found |\n| 4 | Upstream Quote | String | Verbatim quote from the upstream (source/spec) document |\n| 5 | Downstream Quote | String | Verbatim quote from the downstream (generated/roadmap) document |\n| 6 | Impact | String | Assessment of the deviation's impact on correctness or completeness |\n| 7 | Recommended Correction | String | Specific action to resolve the deviation |\n\n### Severity Classification\n\n| Level | Criteria |\n|---|---|\n| HIGH | Functional requirement missing, signature changed, constraint dropped, API contract broken |\n| MEDIUM | Requirement simplified, parameter renamed, NFR softened |\n| LOW | Formatting difference, section reordering, clarification added |\n\n### Source Pair Encoding\n\nThe `Source Pair` information (which two documents were compared) is encoded in the YAML frontmatter:\n\n```yaml\nsource_pair: \"spec.md → roadmap.md\"\nupstream_file: \"spec.md\"\ndownstream_file: \"roadmap.md\"\n```\n\n### Column Name Rationale\n\nGeneric names `Upstream Quote` / `Downstream Quote` are used instead of `Spec Quote` / `Roadmap Quote` because:\n- The fidelity check is reusable across document pairs (spec→roadmap, roadmap→tasklist)\n- Generic names avoid coupling the schema to a specific comparison direction\n- Frontmatter `source_pair` provides the specific document context\n\n## Impacts\n\n- **FR-051.4 AC-2**: This decision ratifies the 7-column schema as canonical.\n- **FR-051.1 AC-5**: The 8-column schema is superseded. (should equal sum of severity counts) |\n| validation_complete | Boolean | `true` if the fidelity check completed without errors |\n| fidelity_check_attempted | Boolean | `true` if the fidelity check was invoked (may be `true` even if validation_complete is `false`) |\n| tasklist_ready | Boolean | `true` only if `high_severity_count == 0` AND `validation_complete == true` |\n\n## Deviation Table Schema (7 Columns)\n\nThe deviation table follows the frontmatter and uses standard Markdown table format:\n\n| # | Column | Type | Description |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| 1 | ID | String | Unique deviation identifier. Format: `DEV-NNN` (zero-padded 3-digit). |\n| 2 | Severity | Enum | One of: `HIGH`, `MEDIUM`, `LOW`. |\n| 3 | Deviation | String | Concise description of what differs between upstream and downstream. |\n| 4 | Upstream Quote | String | Verbatim quote from the upstream document demonstrating the expected content. |\n| 5 | Downstream Quote | String | Verbatim quote from the downstream document showing the actual content (or `[MISSING]` if absent). |\n| 6 | Impact | String | Assessment of how this deviation affects correctness, completeness, or downstream consumers. |\n| 7 | Recommended Correction | String | Specific, actionable instruction to resolve the deviation. |\n\n## Severity Classification Rules\n\n| Level | Criteria | Examples |\n|---|---|---|\n| HIGH | Functional requirement missing, signature changed, constraint dropped, API contract broken | Missing FR, wrong parameter types, deleted validation rule |\n| MEDIUM | Requirement simplified, parameter renamed, NFR softened | Reduced precision, name change without semantic loss, relaxed threshold |\n| LOW | Formatting difference, section reordering, clarification added | Whitespace change, moved paragraph, added explanatory note |\n\n## Gate Interactions\n\n| Gate Check | Field Used | Logic | Blocking |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `_high_severity_count_zero()` | `high_severity_count` | Returns `True` only if value is `0`; `False` if missing | Yes (v2.20) |\n| `_tasklist_ready_consistent()` | `tasklist_ready`, `high_severity_count`, `validation_complete` | Returns `True` if `tasklist_ready` is consistent with `high_severity_count == 0 AND validation_complete == true` | Yes (v2.20) |\n| Count cross-validation | All severity counts vs table rows | Warning log on mismatch; not blocking | No (warning only) |\n\n## Example Report\n\n```markdown\n---\nsource_pair: \"spec.md → roadmap.md\"\nupstream_file: \"spec.md\"\ndownstream_file: \"roadmap.md\"\nhigh_severity_count: 1\nmedium_severity_count: 2\nlow_severity_count: 0\ntotal_deviations: 3\nvalidation_complete: true\nfidelity_check_attempted: true\ntasklist_ready: false\n---\n\n# Deviation Report: spec.md → roadmap.md\n\n| ID | Severity | Deviation | Upstream Quote | Downstream Quote | Impact | Recommended Correction |\n|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|\n| DEV-001 | HIGH | Missing FR-019 implementation | \"Cross-references must be validated\" | [MISSING] | Pipeline cannot enforce cross-ref integrity | Add FR-019 to roadmap Phase 2 deliverables |\n| DEV-002 | MEDIUM | NFR timeout relaxed | \"120s hard limit\" | \"120s target, 600s timeout\" | Performance measurement less strict | Clarify as p95 target per OQ-008 decision |\n| DEV-003 | MEDIUM | Parameter renamed | \"spec_file\" | \"source_file\" | Import paths need updating | Rename to \"spec_file\" for consistency |\n```\n\n## Versioning\n\nThis schema is version 1.0, effective for v2.20 WorkflowEvolution. Changes to the schema require a new decision document updating D-0003 and incrementing this version number.\n","numLines":107,"startLine":1,"totalLines":107}}}

All consumers MUST conform to this schema.\n\n| Field | Value |\n|---|---|\n| Schema Version | 1.0 |\n| Source Decision | D-0003 (OQ-006) |\n| Effective Release | v2.20 WorkflowEvolution |\n\n## YAML Frontmatter\n\nEvery deviation report begins with YAML frontmatter:\n\n```yaml\n---\nsource_pair: \"<upstream_file> → <downstream_file>\"\nupstream_file: \"<path to upstream document>\"\ndownstream_file: \"<path to downstream document>\"\nhigh_severity_count: <integer>\nmedium_severity_count: <integer>\nlow_severity_count: <integer>\ntotal_deviations: <integer>\nvalidation_complete: <boolean>\nfidelity_check_attempted: <boolean>\ntasklist_ready: <boolean>\n---\n```\n\n### Frontmatter Field Definitions\n\n| Field | Type | Required | Description |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `source_pair` | String | Yes | Human-readable label: `\"<upstream> → <downstream>\"` |\n| `upstream_file` | String | Yes | Relative path to the upstream (source/spec) document |\n| `downstream_file` | String | Yes | Relative path to the downstream (generated) document |\n| `high_severity_count` | Integer | Yes | Count of HIGH-severity deviations (≥0) |\n| `medium_severity_count` | Integer | Yes | Count of MEDIUM-severity deviations (≥0) |\n| `low_severity_count` | Integer | Yes | Count of LOW-severity deviations (≥0) |\n| `total_deviations` | Integer | Yes | Total deviation count (must equal sum of severity counts) |\n| `validation_complete` | Boolean | Yes | `true` if the fidelity check completed without errors |\n| `fidelity_check_attempted` | Boolean | Yes | `true` if the fidelity check was invoked |\n| `tasklist_ready` | Boolean | Yes | `true` only if `high_severity_count == 0` AND `validation_complete == true` |\n\n## Deviation Table Schema (7 Columns)\n\nThe deviation table uses standard Markdown table format:\n\n| # | Column | Type | Constraints | Description |\n|---|---|---|---|---|\n| 1 | ID | String | Format: `DEV-NNN` | Unique deviation identifier, zero-padded 3-digit |\n| 2 | Severity | Enum | `HIGH` \\| `MEDIUM` \\| `LOW` | Classification level |\n| 3 | Deviation | String | Non-empty | Concise description of what differs |\n| 4 | Upstream Quote | String | Non-empty | Verbatim quote from upstream document |\n| 5 | Downstream Quote | String | Non-empty or `[MISSING]` | Verbatim quote from downstream document |\n| 6 | Impact | String | Non-empty | Assessment of how deviation affects correctness |\n| 7 | Recommended Correction | String | Non-empty | Specific action to resolve the deviation |\n\n## Column Name Rationale\n\nGeneric names `Upstream Quote` / `Downstream Quote` are used instead of `Spec Quote` / `Roadmap Quote` because the fidelity check is reusable across document pairs (spec→roadmap, roadmap→tasklist). The frontmatter `source_pair` field provides specific document context.\n\n## Gate Interactions\n\n| Gate Check | Field Used | Logic | Blocking in v2.20 |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `_high_severity_count_zero()` | `high_severity_count` | `True` if value is `0`; `False` if missing or >0 | Yes |\n| `_tasklist_ready_consistent()` | `tasklist_ready`, `high_severity_count`, `validation_complete` | `True` if consistent | Yes |\n| Count cross-validation | All severity counts vs table rows | Warning log on mismatch | No (warning only) |\n\n## Example\n\n```markdown\n---\nsource_pair: \"spec.md → roadmap.md\"\nupstream_file: \"spec.md\"\ndownstream_file: \"roadmap.md\"\nhigh_severity_count: 1\nmedium_severity_count: 2\nlow_severity_count: 0\ntotal_deviations: 3\nvalidation_complete: true\nfidelity_check_attempted: true\ntasklist_ready: false\n---\n\n# Deviation Report: spec.md → roadmap.md\n\n| ID | Severity | Deviation | Upstream Quote | Downstream Quote | Impact | Recommended Correction |\n|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|\n| DEV-001 | HIGH | Missing FR-019 | \"Cross-references must be validated\" | [MISSING] | No cross-ref integrity | Add FR-019 to Phase 2 |\n| DEV-002 | MEDIUM | NFR timeout relaxed | \"120s hard limit\" | \"120s target, 600s timeout\" | Less strict measurement | Clarify per OQ-008 |\n| DEV-003 | MEDIUM | Parameter renamed | \"spec_file\" | \"source_file\" | Import paths affected | Rename for consistency |\n```\n\n## Versioning\n\nSchema version 1.0, effective for v2.20. Schema changes require a new decision document and version increment.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2349,"cache_read_input_tokens":124036,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":2349,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":18,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"477530b4-8a69-41e7-93e3-00a493e9664e","uuid":"585dc6e7-53ad-4ebc-ab55-b1abcf98eb59"}

HIGH-severity deviations block pipeline progression in v2.20.\n\n**Criteria**: Functional requirement missing, signature changed, constraint dropped, API contract broken, security control absent.\n\n**Examples**:\n1. A functional requirement specified in the spec (e.g., FR-019 \"Cross-references must be validated\") is entirely absent from the roadmap\n2. An API endpoint's parameter types differ from the spec (e.g., `timeout: int` in spec, `timeout: str` in roadmap)\n3. A security constraint is dropped (e.g., spec requires input sanitization, roadmap omits it)\n\n**Boundary with MEDIUM**: If the requirement is _present but simplified_ (not missing), classify as MEDIUM. If the requirement is _entirely absent or semantically inverted_, classify as HIGH.\n\n### MEDIUM — Non-Blocking Deviations (v2.20)\n\nDeviations that indicate simplification, weakening, or renaming without complete loss. MEDIUM deviations are logged but do not block the pipeline in v2.20 (per OQ-005 / D-0007).\n\n**Criteria**: Requirement simplified, parameter renamed, NFR softened, threshold relaxed, coverage reduced.\n\n**Examples**:\n1. A requirement is simplified: spec says \"retry with exponential backoff and jitter\", roadmap says \"retry on failure\"\n2. A parameter is renamed without semantic loss: `spec_file` → `source_file`\n3. An NFR threshold is relaxed: spec says \"p95 < 100ms\", roadmap says \"p95 < 200ms\"\n\n**Boundary with HIGH**: If the simplification eliminates a _critical constraint_ (e.g., removing retry behavior entirely), classify as HIGH. If the simplification preserves intent but reduces precision, classify as MEDIUM.\n\n**Boundary with LOW**: If the change is purely cosmetic (formatting, ordering) with zero semantic impact, classify as LOW. If the change alters meaning even slightly, classify as MEDIUM.\n\n### LOW — Informational Deviations\n\nDeviations that are cosmetic, organizational, or additive with no semantic impact. LOW deviations are recorded for completeness but have no effect on pipeline behavior.\n\n**Criteria**: Formatting difference, section reordering, clarification added, whitespace change, editorial improvement.\n\n**Examples**:\n1. A section is moved from position 3 to position 5 in the document without changing content\n2. A paragraph is rewritten for clarity but preserves the exact same meaning\n3. Additional explanatory notes are added that do not contradict the spec\n\n**Boundary with MEDIUM**: If the reordering or reformatting changes the _logical grouping_ of requirements (e.g., moving a security requirement out of the security section), classify as MEDIUM.\n\n## Classification Rationale for Prompt Reuse (RSK-007)\n\nWhen embedding severity classification in LLM prompts, include these disambiguation rules:\n\n1. **Missing vs. Simplified**: A requirement that is _absent_ is HIGH; a requirement that is _present but weakened_ is MEDIUM\n2. **Rename vs. Semantic Change**: A parameter _renamed_ without behavioral change is MEDIUM; a parameter whose _type or semantics change_ is HIGH\n3. **Additive vs. Contradictory**: Content _added_ that does not contradict the spec is LOW; content that _contradicts_ the spec is HIGH\n4. **Format vs. Structure**: Pure _formatting_ changes are LOW; _structural reorganization_ that changes logical grouping is MEDIUM\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3853,"cache_read_input_tokens":124346,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":3853,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":2,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"477530b4-8a69-41e7-93e3-00a493e9664e","uuid":"97f168e8-e959-4938-9fee-283cd8dd1a0e"}
